[Shelpies 11:41:00 AM] Velvety tresses cascade down from the top of her head, crowning her in a curtain of pallid locks. Amber insets peer silently ahead of her, uncertainty and confusion written all over her countenance. Melody knows not where she had wandered into, yet the vivid understanding thereto accompanies her much like the veil of mystique that emanates from the core of her being. An otherworldly aura emanates from the center of her being, leading to a seemingly frigid exterior that marks her as a thorny introvert of sorts.

The place that she found herself within, while foreign in terms of structure and actual location, isn't something that she hates admittedly. It is a library of sorts, filled with numerous books that placate her good will. There's no further need for her to be alarmed, if only due to the fact that anywhere with such a ripe collection of books-- all seemingly taken care of, is a place that she could relax within. Yet something perturbs her, and it is instantaneously found out by the pale-haired witch.

She holds her left hand aloft, glancing askance at the brand imprinted on the back of her hand. It glistens and glows with power, yet it does not rival the magical might that she once held in her own world. It instantaneously confirms her presumptions, that her comrades' last-ditch spell worked, and she had been transported elsewhere-- to safety. A pained gasp parts her lips for but an instance, her stoic countenance marred with the vestiges of defeat.

Yet she dwells not on her defeat, and instead lowers her hand to her side. She looks around the area in search for a person to interrogate, or at the very least a subject to observe and derive information from. Gentle footfalls move her out of the aisle betwixt bookshelves, permitting her to stand amidst the library that she had found herself transported into. Silence is eminent from her silent and stoic figure as she looks around, analyzing every single thing around her. Though she herself is not immune to this analysis, thus anyone nearby could derive information from a glance.

Standing at the height of five feet and eight inches, Melody looks to be an average woman in terms of physique alone. Yet that is where the normalcy ends, for better or for worse. Unnaturally pale tresses adorn her head in a long curtain of smooth locks; irises that color of gold, and ones glistening with an odd form of energy, peer at everything around her. As for her attire? She seems to be garbed in rather fashionable clothing: robes in her world that helped with gathering magical energy.

A fur coat of sorts lay heavily above the black dress on her frame. It is conservative, hiding most of her skin and revealing only a portion of it in the form of her neck and face. Her legs are covered in stockings of sorts, completed with a pair of boots that click against the ground with a faint tapping sound every motion that she makes.

For now, she seems relatively peaceful-- if not inquisitive about her whereabouts. Will there be anyone curious enough to approach her?

[Shelpies 5:53:53 PM] Melody '' Eating food. It is a wonder that I seldom experienced back then. ''

Melody admits to such a thing with a faint smile on her countenance. Being given food for nothing in return at the present time, alongside the wonders of being given information and toured around the unfamiliar world is enough to warrant gratitude for Melody. Thus, she stares directly ahead, divulging a small part of her life as her gaze seems to become distant for a scant few seconds.

'' We tended to ration out our meals, for the tyrant kingdom we stood up against had food on lock down. We had to trade with other countries, or farm our own. The latter tends to not end well as we were always on the move. ''

At the end of her long statement, she looks up at the skies with a faint smile of hope on her physiognomy, despite the fact that she's stuck far from those she sought to protect-- from the people that she fought for.

'' That is why once I return home, I will make sure that they taste the same delicacies as I do in this foreign place. ''

Beyond her puerile pretense towards the new and unusual culture around her, Melody no doubt has the heart of a hardened warrior. Nay, beyond that. She is a true rebel, one that fights for a cause that she believed in. One who lived and died for the cause that she rose up for. She clears her throat after the unnecessarily deep statements, with her hand being the first one to establish contact for once.

She places a hand on top of Faye's shoulder.

'' I have not stated these words yet, so allow me to. Thank you for your hospitality, after this, I will search for my accommodations. I cannot impose upon you and your betrothed any further. ''
